<script>
  var url = '/_events/api/setEvent';

  var sendMetrics = function(event, user = {}) {
    var unique_identifier = uuidv4();

    try {
      var data = {
        request: {
          id: unique_identifier,
          environment: 'production'
        },
        store: {
          id: 2709871,
          name: 'Martha Freire Store',
          test_account: false,
          has_meta_app: window.has_meta_app ?? false,
          li_search: true
        },
        device: {
          is_mobile: /Mobi/.test(window.navigator.userAgent),
          user_agent: window.navigator.userAgent,
          ip: '###device_ip###'
        },
        page: {
          host: window.location.hostname,
          path: window.location.pathname,
          search: window.location.search,
          type: 'home',
          title: document.title,
          referrer: document.referrer
        },
        timestamp: '###server_timestamp###',
        user_timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        event,
        origin: 'store'
      };

      if (window.performance) {
        var [timing] = window.performance.getEntriesByType('navigation');

        data['time'] = {
          server_response: Math.round(timing.responseStart - timing.requestStart)
        };
      }

      var _user = {},
          user_email_cookie = $.cookie('user_email'),
          user_data_cookie = $.cookie('LI-UserData');

      if (user_email_cookie) {
        var user_email = decodeURIComponent(user_email_cookie);

        _user['email'] = user_email;
      }

      if (user_data_cookie) {
        var user_data = JSON.parse(user_data_cookie);

        _user['logged'] = user_data.logged;
        _user['id'] = user_data.id ?? undefined;
      }

      $.each(user, function(key, value) {
        _user[key] = value;
      });

      if (!$.isEmptyObject(_user)) {
        data['user'] = _user;
      }

      try {
        var session_identifier = $.cookie('li_session_identifier');

        if (!session_identifier) {
          session_identifier = uuidv4();
        };

        var expiration_date = new Date();

        expiration_date.setTime(expiration_date.getTime() + (30 * 60 * 1000)); // 30 minutos

        $.cookie('li_session_identifier', session_identifier, {
          expires: expiration_date,
          path: '/'
        });

        data['session'] = {
          id: session_identifier
        };
      } catch (err) { }

      try {
        var user_session_identifier = $.cookie('li_user_session_identifier');

        if (!user_session_identifier) {
          user_session_identifier = uuidv4();

          $.cookie('li_user_session_identifier', user_session_identifier, {
            path: '/'
          });
        };

        data['user_session'] = {
          id: user_session_identifier
        };
      } catch (err) { }

      var _cookies = {},
          fbc = $.cookie('_fbc'),
          fbp = $.cookie('_fbp');

      if (fbc) {
        _cookies['fbc'] = fbc;
      }

      if (fbp) {
        _cookies['fbp'] = fbp;
      }

      if (!$.isEmptyObject(_cookies)) {
        data['session']['cookies'] = _cookies;
      }

      try {
        var ab_test_cookie = $.cookie('li_ab_test_running');

        if (ab_test_cookie) {
          var ab_test = JSON.parse(atob(ab_test_cookie));

          if (ab_test.length) {
            data['store']['ab_test'] = ab_test;
          }
        }
      } catch (err) { }

      var _utm = {};

      $.each(sessionStorage, function(key, value) {
        if (key.startsWith('utm_')) {
          var name = key.split('_')[1];

          _utm[name] = value;
        }
      });

      if (!$.isEmptyObject(_utm)) {
        data['session']['utm'] = _utm;
      }

      var controller = new AbortController();

      setTimeout(function() {
        controller.abort();
      }, 5000);

      fetch(url, {
        keepalive: true,
        method: 'POST',
        headers: {
          'Content-Type': 'application/json'
        },
        body: JSON.stringify({ data }),
        signal: controller.signal
      });
    } catch (err) { }

    return unique_identifier;
  }
</script>

    
<script>
  (function() {
    var initABTestHandler = function() {
      try {
        if ($.cookie('li_ab_test_running')) {
          return
        };
        var running_tests = [];

        
        
        
        

        var running_tests_to_cookie = JSON.stringify(running_tests);
        running_tests_to_cookie = btoa(running_tests_to_cookie);
        $.cookie('li_ab_test_running', running_tests_to_cookie, {
          path: '/'
        });

        
        if (running_tests.length > 0) {
          setTimeout(function() {
            $.ajax({
              url: "/conta/status"
            });
          }, 500);
        };

      } catch (err) { }
    }
    setTimeout(initABTestHandler, 500);
  }());
</script>

    
<script>
  $(function() {
    // Clicar em um produto
    $('.listagem-item').click(function() {
      var row, column;

      var $list = $(this).closest('[data-produtos-linha]'),
          index = $(this).closest('li').index();

      if($list.find('.listagem-linha').length === 1) {
        var productsPerRow = $list.data('produtos-linha');

        row = Math.floor(index / productsPerRow) + 1;
        column = (index % productsPerRow) + 1;
      } else {
        row = $(this).closest('.listagem-linha').index() + 1;
        column = index + 1;
      }

      var body = {
        item_id: $(this).attr('data-id'),
        item_sku: $(this).find('.produto-sku').text(),
        item_name: $(this).find('.nome-produto').text().trim(),
        item_row: row,
        item_column: column
      };

      var eventID = sendMetrics({
        type: 'event',
        name: 'select_product',
        data: body
      });

      $(document).trigger('li_select_product', [eventID, body]);
    });

    // Clicar no "Fale Conosco"
    $('#modalContato').on('show', function() {
      var value = 'Fale Conosco';

      var eventID = sendMetrics({
        type: 'event',
        name: 'start_contact',
        data: { text: value }
      });

      $(document).trigger('li_start_contact', [eventID, value]);
    });

    // Clicar no WhatsApp
    $('.li-whatsapp a').click(function() {
      var value = 'WhatsApp';

      var eventID = sendMetrics({
        type: 'event',
        name: 'start_contact',
        data: { text: value }
      });

      $(document).trigger('li_start_contact', [eventID, value]);
    });

    
      // Visualizar a página inicial
      var eventID = sendMetrics({
        type: 'pageview',
        name: 'view_home'
      });

      $(document).trigger('li_view_home', [eventID]);
    
  });
</script>

      <script>
        var is_full_page_loading = true;
        function removePageLoading() {
          if (is_full_page_loading) {
            try {
              $('#full-page-loading').remove();
            } catch(e) {}
            try {
              var div_loading = document.getElementById('full-page-loading');
              if (div_loading) {
                div_loading.remove();
              };
            } catch(e) {}
            is_full_page_loading = false;
          };
        };
        $(function() {
          setTimeout(function() {
            removePageLoading();
          }, 1);
        });
      </script>

                    <div class="span4 sobre-loja-rodape">
  <span class="titulo">Sobre a loja</span>
  <p>
      A Martha é uma empresa focada em vestuário feminino

Trabalhamos para ajudar os nossos clientes a encontrar o seu look perfeito, seguinte a suas exigências, pois conhecemos o potencial dela e sabemos como utilizá-la a favor dos nossos clientes, para que assim os mesmos se sinta realizado ao utilizar os nossos produtos. Nossa empresa nasceu em 2012 como loja física de moda feminina na região metropolitana do estado de São Paulo, oferecendo roupas de Confecção Própria e Marcas Nacionais renomadas.
  </p>
</div>

          <script type="text/javascript">
      var hasInitializedGoogleAuth = false;
      var btnsAuthGoogle = $('.button-auth-google');

      function urlToValidate(fromOneTap = false) {
        var actualUrl = new URL(window.location.href);
        var next = actualUrl.searchParams.get('next');

        if (!next) {
          if (!btnsAuthGoogle.is(':visible'))
            next = actualUrl.pathname


          if (!fromOneTap && btnsAuthGoogle.eq(0).hasClass('to-checkout'))
            next = '/checkout'

          if (actualUrl.pathname.includes('checkout'))
            next = actualUrl.pathname
        }

        actualUrl.searchParams.append('metodo', 'google');
        if (!next) {
          actualUrl.searchParams.append('next', '/conta/index' + actualUrl.search);
        } else {
          actualUrl.searchParams.delete('next');
          actualUrl.searchParams.append('next', next + actualUrl.search);
        }
        actualUrl.searchParams.delete('metodo');
        return 'https://www.marthafreirestore.com.br/conta/login/google' + actualUrl.search
      }

      function addGsiScript(callbackOnLoadGsi) {
        if (!document.getElementById('script_gsi')) {
          const script = document.createElement('script');
          script.src = 'https://accounts.google.com/gsi/client';
          script.id = 'script_gsi';
          script.async = true;
          script.defer = true;
          script.addEventListener('load', callbackOnLoadGsi);
          document.body.appendChild(script);
        }
      }

      function renderGoogleAuthButtons() {
        if (btnsAuthGoogle.length > 0) {
          btnsAuthGoogle.each(function() {
            var rendered = $(this).data('rendered') || false;
            var action = $(this).data('action');
            var width = parseInt("220") || 200;
            if (!rendered) {
              google.accounts.id.renderButton(
                this,
                {
                  type: "standard",
                  shape: "pill",
                  theme: "outline",
                  text: action,
                  size: "large",
                  width,
                }
              );
              $(this).data('rendered', true);
            }
          });
        }
      }

      function onSuccessGoogleAuth(data) {
        const ot_form = document.createElement('form');
        const fromOnetap = data.hasOwnProperty('select_by') && !data.select_by.includes('btn');
        ot_form.id = 'google_auth';
        ot_form.action = urlToValidate(fromOnetap);
        ot_form.method = 'POST';
        for (let item in data) {
            const input = document.createElement('input');
            input.type = 'hidden';
            input.name = item;
            input.value = data[item];
            ot_form.appendChild(input);
        }
        document.body.appendChild(ot_form);
        ot_form.submit();
      }

      function initializeGoogleAuth(withOneTap = false) {
        if (!hasInitializedGoogleAuth && (btnsAuthGoogle.length > 0 || withOneTap)) {
          function callbackOnLoadGsi() {
            var params = {
              client_id: '385166315128-21631bsbvhj3je807i9e1c7pp1rskgik.apps.googleusercontent.com',
              context: 'signin',
              ux_mode: 'popup',
              callback: onSuccessGoogleAuth,
              login_uri: urlToValidate(),
            }

            if (withOneTap) {
              params['itp_support'] = true
              params['cancel_on_tap_outside'] = false
            }

            google.accounts.id.initialize(params);
            hasInitializedGoogleAuth = true;

            if (btnsAuthGoogle.length > 0) {
              renderGoogleAuthButtons();
            }

            if (withOneTap && !btnsAuthGoogle.is(':visible')) {
              google.accounts.id.prompt();
            }
          }
          addGsiScript(callbackOnLoadGsi);
        }
      }

      
        
            $(function() {
              if (!btnsAuthGoogle.is(':visible')) {
                
                  $('body').on('user_state_changed', function(e, params) {
                    var isLogged = (params && params.logged) || false;
                    if (!isLogged) {
                      initializeGoogleAuth(true);
                    }
                  });
                
              } else {
                initializeGoogleAuth();
              }
            });
        
      
    </script>
        
      
        
          
        
      
    

    

    
	<!-- Video Home JS -->
  
      <!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="pt-BR">
<head>
  <meta charset="UTF-8" />
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0"/>
  <title>Slider com Splide e Lazy Loading</title>
  <!-- CSS do Splide -->
  <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/@splidejs/splide/dist/css/splide.min.css" />
  <link rel="stylesheet" href="estilo-slider.css" />
</head>
<body>
  <div id="bv">
    <h2 class="tc"><strong>Mais Vistos</strong></h2>
    <p class="subtitulo">Toque Para Ver o Vídeo</p>
    <div id="splide" class="splide">
      <div class="splide__track">
        <ul id="splideList" class="splide__list"></ul>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div class="vp" id="vp">
      <div class="vpc">
        <span class="cb" id="cp">&times;</span>
        <video class="fv" id="fv" playsinline webkit-playsinline preload="auto"></video>
        <button class="bn" id="bn">VER PROMOÇÃO</button>
      </div>

  <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/@splidejs/splide/dist/js/splide.min.js"></script>
  <script>
    const SLIDES_PER_PAGE = 3;
    const AUTO_INTERVAL   = 15000;
    const mappingUrl      = 'https://raw.githubusercontent.com/marthafreirestore1/video/refs/heads/main/videos.html';
    const currentPath     = window.location.pathname + window.location.search;

    // ─── fetchCached genérico ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    const _fetchCache = new Map();
    function fetchCached(url, options) {
      if (!_fetchCache.has(url)) {
        const p = fetch(url, options)
          .then(res => {
            if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Falha ao buscar ${url}: ${res.status}`);
            return res.text();
          });
        _fetchCache.set(url, p);
      }
      return _fetchCache.get(url);
    }

    // ─── Obter mapeamento de vídeos ───────────────────────────────────────────────
    function fetchMappingData(url) {
      return fetchCached(url)
        .then(html => {
          const doc  = new DOMParser().parseFromString(html, 'text/html');
          const rows = doc.querySelectorAll('table tbody tr:not(:first-child)');
          const mappings = [];
          rows.forEach(row => {
            const cells = row.querySelectorAll('td');
            mappings.push({
              link:       cells[0].textContent.trim(),
              videoFull:  cells[1].textContent.trim(),
              videoThumb: cells[2].textContent.trim(),
              usar:       cells[3].textContent.trim().toLowerCase(),
              nome:       cells[4].textContent.trim(),
            });
          });
          return mappings;
        });
    }

    // ─── Construir slides no Splide ──────────────────────────────────────────────
    function buildSlides(mappings) {
      const list = document.getElementById('splideList');
      mappings.forEach(item => {
        if (item.usar === 's') {
          const li = document.createElement('li');
          li.className = 'splide__slide';
          li.innerHTML = `
            <div class="slide-content ci"
                 data-video-full="${item.videoFull}"
                 data-buy-link="${item.link}">
              <div class="c">
                <video class="mv"
                       data-src="${item.videoThumb}"
                       muted autoplay loop
                       playsinline webkit-playsinline
                       preload="auto"></video>
              </div>
              <p class="dt">${item.nome}</p>
            </div>`;
          list.appendChild(li);
        }
      });
    }

    // ─── Lazy load e controle de play/pause de vídeos em miniatura ──────────────
    function setupObservers() {
      const options = { root: null, rootMargin: '0px', threshold: 0.1 };
      const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries, obs) => {
        entries.forEach(entry => {
          const video = entry.target;
          // lazy load src
          if (entry.isIntersecting) {
            if (video.dataset.src && !video.src) {
              video.src = video.dataset.src;
            }
            // play quando entra no viewport
            video.play().catch(() => {});
          } else {
            // pause quando sai do viewport
            video.pause();
          }
          // após carregar e iniciar, desanexa se não precisar mais observar
          if (video.src === video.dataset.src) {
            obs.observe(video);
          }
        });
      }, options);

      document.querySelectorAll('video.mv').forEach(video => {
        observer.observe(video);
      });
    }

    // ─── Inicialização ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
      // insere o contêiner antes do alvo
      const b      = document.getElementById('bv');
      const target = document.querySelector('.conteiner .row-fluid .titulo-categoria.vitrine-mas-vendido');
      if (b && target) target.parentNode.insertBefore(b, target);

      const vp = document.getElementById('vp');
      const fv = document.getElementById('fv');
      const cp = document.getElementById('cp');
      const bn = document.getElementById('bn');

      fetchMappingData(mappingUrl).then(mappings => {
        buildSlides(mappings);
        const splide = new Splide('#splide', {
          type:        'loop',
          autoplay:    true,
          interval:    AUTO_INTERVAL,
          pauseOnHover:false,
          perPage:     SLIDES_PER_PAGE,
          gap:         '10px',
          breakpoints: { 1024: { perPage: SLIDES_PER_PAGE }, 768: { perPage: SLIDES_PER_PAGE } },
        });
        splide.mount();

        // ajusta observers após montar
        setupObservers();

        // clique nas miniaturas
        document.querySelectorAll('.ci').forEach(sl => {
          sl.addEventListener('click', () => {
            const vf = sl.getAttribute('data-video-full');
            const bl = sl.getAttribute('data-buy-link');
            fv.src = vf;
            vp.style.display = 'flex';
            fv.play();
            history.pushState(null, null, '#popupvideo');
            bn.onclick = () => window.location.href = bl;
          });
        });
      });

      // fechar popup
      function closePopup() {
        vp.style.display = 'none';
        fv.pause();
        fv.removeAttribute('src');
        fv.load();
        history.pushState(null, null, currentPath);
      }
      cp.addEventListener('click', closePopup);
      vp.addEventListener('click', e => { if (e.target === vp) closePopup(); });
      window.addEventListener('popstate', () => {
        if (location.hash !== '#popupvideo') closePopup();
      });
    });
  </script>
</body>
</html>

  

	<!-- Video Vitrine JS -->
  
    <script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
      
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    // ─── Cache genérico de fetch por URL ─────────────────────────────────────
    const _fetchCache = new Map();
    function fetchCached(url, options) {
      if (!_fetchCache.has(url)) {
        const p = fetch(url, options)
          .then(res => {
            if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Falha ao buscar ${url}: ${res.status}`);
            return res.text();
          });
        _fetchCache.set(url, p);
      }
      return _fetchCache.get(url);
    }

    // ─── Vídeo na vitrine (somente ofertas) ─────────────────────────────────
    let videoMapPromise = null;
    function fetchVideoMap() {
      if (!videoMapPromise) {
        videoMapPromise = fetchCached(
          'https://raw.githubusercontent.com/marthafreirestore1/video/refs/heads/main/videos.html'
        )
        .then(html => {
          const doc  = new DOMParser().parseFromString(html, 'text/html');
          return Array.from(doc.querySelectorAll('table tbody tr:not(:first-child)'))
            .reduce((map, tr) => {
              const [tdPath,, tdVideo, tdUse] = tr.querySelectorAll('td');
              const page = tdPath?.textContent.trim();
              const url2 = tdVideo?.textContent.trim();
              if (page && url2 && tdUse.textContent.trim().toUpperCase() === 'S') {
                map[page] = url2;
              }
              return map;
            }, {});
        })
        .catch(err => {
          console.error('Erro ao carregar vídeo‑map:', err);
          return {};
        });
      }
      return videoMapPromise;
    }

    function injectVideos() {
      const ofertasSection = document.querySelector('.vitrine-ofertas.item-home');
      if (!ofertasSection) return;

      fetchVideoMap().then(videoMap => {
        let count = 0, MAX = 15;

        const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
          entries.forEach(entry => {
            const vid = entry.target;
            const url = vid.dataset.src;
            if (!url) {
              observer.unobserve(vid);
              return;
            }
            if (entry.isIntersecting) {
              if (!vid.src) vid.src = url;
              vid.play().catch(() => {});
            } else {
              vid.pause();
            }
          });
        }, {
          root: ofertasSection,
          threshold: 0.1
        });

        ofertasSection
          .querySelectorAll('.listagem-item-wrap, .listagem-item')
          .forEach(item => {
            if (count >= MAX) return;

            const container = item.querySelector('.imagem-produto');
            if (!container || container.querySelector('video.lazy-video')) return;

            const link = item.querySelector('a.produto-sobrepor, a.nome-produto');
            if (!link?.href) return;

            const page = new URL(link.href).pathname;
            const url2 = videoMap[page];
            if (!url2) return;

            const { width: W, height: H } = container.getBoundingClientRect();
            const img = container.querySelector('img.imagem-principal');
            if (img) img.remove();

            const wrap = document.createElement('div');
            wrap.className = 'video-wrapper';
            wrap.style.width  = `${W}px`;
            wrap.style.height = `${H}px`;

            const vid = document.createElement('video');
            vid.dataset.src   = url2;
            vid.preload       = 'metadata';
            vid.autoplay      = false;
            vid.loop          = true;
            vid.playsInline   = true;
            vid.muted         = true;
            vid.volume        = 0;
            vid.className     = 'video-vitrine lazy-video';

            wrap.appendChild(vid);
            container.appendChild(wrap);

            observer.observe(vid);
            count++;
          });
      });
    }

    // dispara injeção de vídeos em eventos e mutações
    ['DOMContentLoaded','load','splide:mounted','splide:updated']
      .forEach(evt => document.addEventListener(evt, injectVideos));

    // registra o MutationObserver *após* o DOM estar pronto
    const ofertasRoot = document.querySelector('.vitrine-ofertas.item-home');
    if (ofertasRoot) {
      new MutationObserver(injectVideos).observe(ofertasRoot, {
        childList: true,
        subtree:   true,
      });
    }
  });

    </script>
  

	<!-- [Config] Functions -->
  
    <script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
      // Função para definir cookie
function setCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
    var d = new Date();
    d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays*24*60*60*1000));
    var expires = "expires="+ d.toUTCString();
    document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
}

// Função para ler cookie
function getCookie(cname) {
    var name = cname + "=";
    var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
    var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
    for(var i = 0; i <ca.length; i++) {
        var c = ca[i];
        while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
            c = c.substring(1);
        }
        if (c.indexOf(name) === 0) {
            return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
        }
    }
    return "";
}
    </script>

      <!-- Ajustes de CSS para o launcher do Tawk.to -->
<style>
  .widget-visible > iframe:first-of-type,
  html.tawk-mobile .tawk-min-chat-icon {
    transform-origin: bottom right !important;
    transform: scale(0.8) translateX(-20px) !important;
  }
</style>

<script>
(function(){
  function ajustarLauncher(){
    const path = window.location.pathname.toLowerCase();
    const shouldHide = path.includes('carrinho');

    const lf = document.querySelector('.widget-visible > iframe:first-of-type');
    if (lf) {
      if (shouldHide) {
        lf.style.display = 'none';
      } else {
        lf.style.display        = '';
        lf.style.bottom         = '14px';
        lf.style.width          = '40px';
        lf.style.height         = '40px';
        lf.style.transform      = 'scale(0.8) translateX(-20px)';
        lf.style.transformOrigin= 'bottom right';
      }
    }

    const icon = document.querySelector('.tawk-min-chat-icon');
    if (icon) {
      if (shouldHide) {
        icon.style.display = 'none';
      } else {
        icon.style.display        = '';
        icon.style.width          = '24px';
        icon.style.height         = '24px';
        icon.style.transform      = 'scale(0.8) translateX(-20px)';
        icon.style.transformOrigin= 'bottom right';
      }
    }
  }

  // Ganchos oficiais do Tawk.to
  window.Tawk_API = window.Tawk_API || {};
  ['onLoad', 'onChatMaximized', 'onChatMinimized'].forEach(evt => {
    window.Tawk_API[evt] = () => {
      if (evt === 'onChatMinimized') {
        setTimeout(ajustarLauncher, 50);
      } else {
        ajustarLauncher();
      }
    };
  });

  // Fallback robusto: observa recriações do iframe/ícone
  const observer = new MutationObserver(ajustarLauncher);
  observer.observe(document.body, { childList: true, subtree: true });
  setTimeout(() => observer.disconnect(), 10000);

  // (Opcional) seu setInterval original
  let tries = 0;
  const iv = setInterval(() => {
    ajustarLauncher();
    if (++tries > 10) clearInterval(iv);
  }, 500);
})();
</script>

    s1.async=true;
    s1.src='https://embed.tawk.to/5e62a13a8d24fc22658639a3/1iqnjruqt';
    s1.charset='UTF-8';
    s1.setAttribute('crossorigin','*');
    s0.parentNode.insertBefore(s1,s0);
  })();
</script>

  <aside id="mf-sidebar" aria-hidden="true">

    </div>
    <div class="mf-header">

      <button id="mf-close-btn" aria-label="Fechar">×</button>
    </div>
    <div class="mf-tabs">

      <button data-tab="esgotando">Quase Esgotando</button>
    </div>

      <ul id="mf-desejos" class="mf-list active"></ul>
      <ul id="mf-esgotando" class="mf-list"></ul>

  <script>
  ;(function(){
    const MAP_URL       = 'https://raw.githubusercontent.com/marthafreirestore1/video/refs/heads/main/visitantes.html';
    const MAP_CACHE_KEY = 'mf_mapData';
    const MAP_TS_KEY    = 'mf_mapTS';
    const MAP_TTL       = 12 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // 12h
    const VIS_TTL       = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // 24h
    let isLoaded        = false;
    let mapData         = [];

    async function loadMap(){
      const now  = Date.now();
      const last = parseInt(localStorage.getItem(MAP_TS_KEY),10) || 0;
      if(now - last < MAP_TTL){
        mapData = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(MAP_CACHE_KEY) || '[]');
        return;
      }
      const html = await fetch(MAP_URL).then(r=> r.text());
      const tmp  = document.createElement('div');
      tmp.innerHTML = html;
      mapData = Array.from(tmp.querySelectorAll('tbody tr')).map(tr=>{
        const td = tr.querySelectorAll('td');
        return {
          link:  td[0]?.textContent.trim()  || '',
          name:  td[1]?.textContent.trim()  || '',
          thumb: td[2]?.textContent.trim()  || '',
          old:   td[3]?.textContent.trim()  || '',
          neo:   td[4]?.textContent.trim()  || '',
          sep:   parseInt(td[5]?.textContent.trim(),10) || null,
          esg:   parseInt(td[7]?.textContent.trim(),10) || null
        };
      });
      localStorage.setItem(MAP_CACHE_KEY, JSON.stringify(mapData));
      localStorage.setItem(MAP_TS_KEY, now.toString());
    }

    function getVisited(){
      const raw = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('mf_visited') || '[]');
      const now = Date.now();
      return raw.filter(i=> now - i.ts < VIS_TTL);
    }
    function setVisited(slug){
      const now = Date.now();
      let arr = getVisited().filter(i=> i.slug !== slug);
      arr.unshift({ slug, ts: now });
      localStorage.setItem('mf_visited', JSON.stringify(arr));
    }

    function buildList(items){
      const frag = document.createDocumentFragment();
      items.forEach(p=>{
        const li = document.createElement('li');
        li.innerHTML = `
          <img src="${p.thumb}" alt="${p.name}" loading="lazy">
          <div class="info">
            <h3>${p.name}</h3>
            <div>
              <span class="price-old">${p.old}</span>
              <span class="price-new">${p.neo}</span>
            </div>
            <a href="${p.link}" class="btn-buy">Ver Mais</a>
          </div>`;
        frag.appendChild(li);
      });
      return frag;
    }

    async function openSidebar(){
      sidebar.classList.add('open');
      overlay.classList.add('show');
      if(!isLoaded){
        await loadMap();
        const me = location.pathname;
        if(mapData.some(p=> p.link === me)) setVisited(me);
        const visSlugs = getVisited().map(v=> v.slug);
        const des = visSlugs.map(s=> mapData.find(p=> p.link===s)).filter(Boolean);
        const esg = mapData.filter(p=> p.esg!==null).sort((a,b)=> a.esg-b.esg);
        document.getElementById('mf-desejos').appendChild(buildList(des));
        document.getElementById('mf-esgotando').appendChild(buildList(esg));
        isLoaded = true;
      }
    }
    function closeSidebar(){
      sidebar.classList.remove('open');
      overlay.classList.remove('show');
    }

    const sidebar = document.getElementById('mf-sidebar');
    const overlay = document.getElementById('mf-overlay');
    const btn     = document.getElementById('mf-float-btn');
    const close   = document.getElementById('mf-close-btn');
    const tabs    = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('#mf-sidebar .mf-tabs button'));
    const lists   = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('#mf-sidebar .mf-list'));

    btn.addEventListener('click', openSidebar);
    close.addEventListener('click', closeSidebar);
    overlay.addEventListener('click', closeSidebar);

    tabs.forEach(tab=>{
      tab.addEventListener('click', ()=>{
        tabs.forEach(t=> t.classList.remove('active'));
        lists.forEach(l=> l.classList.remove('active'));
        tab.classList.add('active');
        document.getElementById('mf-'+tab.dataset.tab).classList.add('active');
      });
    });

  })();
  </script>
</body>
</html>

  <!-- Biblioteca de confete -->
  <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/canvas-confetti@1.5.1/dist/confetti.browser.min.js"></script>
  <script>
  (function(){
    const STORAGE_KEY = 'roleta_claim_timestamp';
    const TWO_HOURS   = 2 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // ms

    const floatBtn = document.getElementById('float-button');
    const overlay  = document.getElementById('overlay');
    const popup    = document.getElementById('wheel-popup');
    const closeBtn = document.getElementById('close-btn');
    const spinBtn  = document.getElementById('spin-button');
    const resultD  = document.getElementById('result');
    const timerD   = document.getElementById('timer');
    const claimBtn = document.getElementById('claim-button');
    const wheelEl  = document.getElementById('wheel');
    const canvas   = document.getElementById('wheel-canvas');

    // Segments & Colors
    const segments = [
      'NADA','FRETE GRÁTIS','NADA','4% OFF',
      'NADA','4% OFF','NADA','3% OFF'
    ];
    const colors = [
      '#3D2C29','#30a77e','#3D2C29','#8ACFC7',
      '#3D2C29','#CFC5AF','#3D2C29','#f98087'
    ];
    const preselected = [1];

    // Canvas Hi‑DPI
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio||1;
    const size = 300;
    canvas.width  = size * dpr;
    canvas.height = size * dpr;
    ctx.scale(dpr,dpr);

    function drawWheel(){
      const cx=size/2, cy=size/2, num=segments.length, ang=2*Math.PI/num;
      ctx.clearRect(0,0,size,size);
      for(let i=0;i<num;i++){
        const start=-Math.PI/2 + i*ang, end=start+ang;
        ctx.fillStyle = colors[i];
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(cx,cy);
        ctx.arc(cx,cy,cx,start,end); ctx.fill();
        ctx.strokeStyle='#fff'; ctx.lineWidth=2; ctx.stroke();
        const mid = start + ang/2;
        ctx.save(); ctx.translate(cx,cy); ctx.rotate(mid);
        ctx.fillStyle='#fff'; ctx.font='600 14px Inter';
        ctx.textAlign='center'; ctx.textBaseline='middle';
        ctx.fillText(segments[i], cx*0.65, 0);
        ctx.restore();
      }
    }
    function createPins(){
      const rect=canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
      const cx=rect.width/2, cy=rect.height/2, r=cx;
      for(let i=0;i<6;i++){
        const el=document.createElement('div');
        el.className='pin';
        const ang=-Math.PI/2 + i*(2*Math.PI/6);
        el.style.left = cx + Math.cos(ang)*(r+4)-5 + 'px';
        el.style.top  = cy + Math.sin(ang)*(r+4)-5 + 'px';
        wheelEl.appendChild(el);
      }
    }
    function openPopup(){
      overlay.style.display='block';
      popup.style.display='block';
      drawWheel();
      createPins();
    }
    function closeAll(){
      overlay.style.display='none';
      popup.style.display='none';
    }

    // Verifica cache
    const lastClaim = parseInt(localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY),10);
    if(lastClaim && (Date.now() - lastClaim < TWO_HOURS)) {
      floatBtn.style.display='none';
    }

    floatBtn.addEventListener('click', ()=>{
      openPopup();
      floatBtn.style.display='none';
    });
    closeBtn.addEventListener('click', closeAll);
    overlay.addEventListener('click', closeAll);

    // Spin
    spinBtn.addEventListener('click', ()=>{
      spinBtn.remove();
      const dur    = Math.random()*3 + 4;
      const target = preselected[Math.floor(Math.random()*preselected.length)];
      const full   = 4 + Math.floor(Math.random()*3);
      const deg    = 360/segments.length;
      const offset = 90 - (target*deg + deg/2);
      const final  = full*360 + offset;

      canvas.style.transform = `rotate(${final}deg)`;
      canvas.style.transition = `transform ${dur}s cubic-bezier(.18,.85,.3,1)`;

      canvas.addEventListener('transitionend', function end(){
        canvas.removeEventListener('transitionend', end);
        wheelEl.classList.add('animate-up');
        resultD.textContent = 'Você ganhou: ' + segments[target];
        resultD.style.display = 'block';

        // === Início do timer flip‑clock ===
        timerD.style.display = 'block';
        let remaining = 9 * 60 + 37;
        function pad(n){ return n.toString().padStart(2,'0'); }
        document.getElementById('hours').textContent   = pad(Math.floor(remaining / 3600));
        document.getElementById('minutes').textContent = pad(Math.floor((remaining % 3600) / 60));
        document.getElementById('seconds').textContent = pad(remaining % 60);

        const iv = setInterval(()=>{
          if(remaining <= 0){
            clearInterval(iv);
            document.querySelector('#timer .timer-header').textContent = 'EXPIRADO';
            return;
          }
          remaining--;
          const hrs = Math.floor(remaining / 3600);
          const mins = Math.floor((remaining % 3600) / 60);
          const secs = remaining % 60;
          document.getElementById('hours').textContent   = pad(hrs);
          document.getElementById('minutes').textContent = pad(mins);
          document.getElementById('seconds').textContent = pad(secs);
        }, 1000);
        // === Fim do timer flip‑clock ===

        claimBtn.style.display = 'inline-block';
        claimBtn.addEventListener('click', ()=>{
          confetti({
            particleCount: 200,
            angle:        90,
            spread:      120,
            startVelocity: 65,
            gravity:      0.3,
            ticks:       400,
            decay:       0.8,
            origin: { x: 0.5, y: 0.6 }
          });
          clearInterval(iv);
          localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, Date.now());
          // === Toast frete grátis ===
          const toast = document.createElement('div');
          toast.className = 'free-shipping-toast';
          toast.innerHTML  = 'Frete Grátis Aplicado no Carrinho<br>Agora é só adicionar o produto no carrinho.';
          document.body.appendChild(toast);
          requestAnimationFrame(() => toast.classList.add('show'));
          setTimeout(() => {
            toast.classList.remove('show');
            setTimeout(() => document.body.removeChild(toast), 300);
          }, 7000);
          // === Fim toast ===
          setTimeout(closeAll, 10);
        }, { once: true });

      }, { once: true });
    });

  })();
  </script>
</body>
</html>

	<!-- Avaliação Miniatura JS -->
  
    <script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    // ─── Cache genérico de fetch por URL ────────────────────────────────────────
    const _fetchCache = new Map();
    function fetchCached(url, options) {
      if (!_fetchCache.has(url)) {
        const promise = fetch(url, options)
          .then(res => {
            if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Falha ao buscar ${url}: ${res.status}`);
            return res.text();
          });
        _fetchCache.set(url, promise);
      }
      return _fetchCache.get(url);
    }

    // ─── Core de injeção de sumários ─────────────────────────────────────────────
    let reviewsMap = {};

    function injectSummaries() {
      document.querySelectorAll('.listagem-item-wrap').forEach(item => {
        if (item.querySelector('.rating-summary-small')) return;

        const link = item.querySelector('a.produto-sobrepor') 
                  || item.querySelector('a.nome-produto');
        if (!link?.href) return;

        const pathname = new URL(link.href).pathname;
        const prodStars = reviewsMap[pathname] || [];
        if (!prodStars.length) return;

        const sum = prodStars.reduce((acc, s) => acc + s, 0);
        const avg = (sum / prodStars.length).toFixed(1);

        const summary = document.createElement('div');
        summary.className = 'rating-summary-small';
        summary.innerHTML = `
          <span class="nota">${avg} de 5</span>
          <span class="stars">
            ${[1,2,3,4,5].map(i =>
              `<i class="star ${i <= Math.round(avg) ? 'full' : 'empty'}">★</i>`
            ).join('')}
          </span>
          <span class="count">(${prodStars.length})</span>
        `;

        const infoBox = item.querySelector('.info-produto.prodTxt-2');
        if (infoBox && infoBox.parentNode) {
          infoBox.parentNode.insertBefore(summary, infoBox);
        }
      });
    }

    // ─── Fetch inicial das avaliações ───────────────────────────────────────────
    fetchCached('https://raw.githubusercontent.com/marthafreirestore1/video/refs/heads/main/avaliacoes.html')
      .then(html => {
        const doc  = new DOMParser().parseFromString(html, 'text/html');
        const rows = Array.from(doc.querySelectorAll('table tbody tr:not(:first-child)'));
        reviewsMap = rows.reduce((map, tr) => {
          const page  = tr.children[0].textContent.trim();
          const stars = +tr.children[1].textContent.trim();
          if (!map[page]) map[page] = [];
          map[page].push(stars);
          return map;
        }, {});
        // já injetar ao fim do fetch
        injectSummaries();
      })
      .catch(console.error);

    // ─── Registro de disparadores ───────────────────────────────────────────────
    ['load','splide:mounted','splide:updated'].forEach(evt =>
      document.addEventListener(evt, injectSummaries)
    );

    // ─── Observer para elementos dinâmicos e SPAs ──────────────────────────────
    new MutationObserver(injectSummaries).observe(document.body, {
      childList: true,
      subtree:   true,
    });
  });
    </script>
  


    

    <script>
      window.fbAsyncInit = function() {
        if($('meta[property="fb:app_id"]').length) {
          FB.init({
            appId      : $('meta[property="fb:app_id"]').attr('content'),
            xfbml      : true,
            version    : 'v2.5'
          });
        } else {
          FB.init({
            xfbml      : true,
            version    : 'v2.5'
          });
        }
      };

      (function(d, s, id){
        var js, fjs = d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0];
        if (d.getElementById(id)) {return;}
        js = d.createElement(s); js.id = id;
        js.src = "//connect.facebook.net/pt_BR/sdk.js";
        fjs.parentNode.insertBefore(js, fjs);
      }(document, 'script', 'facebook-jssdk'));
    </script>

    


  
  
    <script type="text/javascript">
      if('serviceWorker' in navigator) {
        window.addEventListener('load', function() {
          navigator.serviceWorker.register('/service-worker.js');
        });
      }
    </script>
  


  </body>
</html>
